## HOW TO START A NEW SESSION

1. Run `th` in Terminal — reads CLAUDE.md and copies to clipboard
2. Open claude.ai → New conversation
3. Paste the opener below, fill in CURRENT ISSUE from clipboard

```
PROJECT: Treehouse Finds — Zen-Forged/treehouse-treasure-search — app.kentuckytreehouse.com
STACK: Next.js 14 App Router · TypeScript · Tailwind · Framer Motion · Anthropic SDK · Supabase · SerpAPI · Vercel
Filesystem MCP is connected at /Users/davidbutler/Projects/treehouse-treasure-search
Read CLAUDE.md, CONTEXT.md, and docs/DECISION_GATE.md. Then run the session opening standup from MASTER_PROMPT.md.

CURRENT ISSUE:
[paste here]
```

## HOW TO END A SESSION

Run `/session-close` — replaces the old `thc` alias with the full close protocol (tombstoning, memory updates, commit + push, PR creation).

## TERMINAL COMMAND FORMATTING CONVENTION
> When Claude surfaces multiple terminal commands to run in sequence, each goes in its own fenced block. This lets David copy one at a time and verify each before running the next.

**Do this:**

```bash
npm run build 2>&1 | tail -30
```

```bash
git add -A && git commit -m "..." && git push
```

**Not this** (chained separate commands in one block that invite blind paste):

```bash
npm run build 2>&1 | tail -30
git add -A && git commit -m "..." && git push
```

Exception: a single chained command with `&&` stays in one block — that's one atomic action by design.

## ✅ Session 170 (2026-05-17) — /find/[id] destination hero design-pass + 4-arc Shape B ship — 5 runtime commits + 1 close

David opened with `/session-open`; standup recommended iPhone QA on production v0.169.0. David redirected to a design ask on `/find/[id]` surfacing **4 concerns**: (1) save/unsave Remove Flag CTA visually identical to secondary Explore Booth button — toggle-state vocabulary collides with action vocabulary; (2) "Purchase this item at" eyebrow reads weak vs dominant title + price block above — text trails off; (3) mall + booth + map should be one component (a secondary hero — "this is where you go to get this item"); (4) overall cohesion — page reads as add-on elements, not one cohesive composition; explicitly "open to recommendations" on item 4. Per `feedback_visibility_tools_first` ✅ Promoted, audit-first parallel read of `app/find/[id]/page.tsx` confirmed root cause: items 1–3 are direct consequences of session 169 round 2's additive ship (CTA pair + standalone map snapshot landed as separate refinements). Item 4 is the synthesis question once they stack up. Per `feedback_triage_cost_shape_before_design_pass` ✅ Promoted, surfaced 3 cost shapes A surgical / B re-architect / C full redesign. David picked **Shape B — re-architect destination as secondary hero**.

### Pre-V1 prose pass (per `feedback_pre_mockup_prose_model_first` ✅ Promoted at session 167)

David's prose direction was clear on items 1–3 + exploratory on item 4. Surfaced 3 prose Qs before V1 (CTA inside hero / carousel disposition / save bubble corner). **David picked Q1 = no CTA inside hero** with significant reframe: *"since it's a /find page the main CTA of the whole page is to Flag the Find. The map really acts as a clear signal to know where it's located and that they can find it. They should be able to click on the map though and it should open the map view on the explore page."* That changed the destination hero from "action-driving anchor" to "purely informational." Q2 = retire "More from this booth" carousel entirely. Q3 = save bubble top-right corner (lattice canonical). Restated implications + flagged load-bearing consequence: Flag the Find moves from full-width primary green button → corner bubble = significant visual weight reduction for what is now the page's primary CTA. Surfaced 1 more prose Q on save bubble visual weight. **David picked standard 44×44 v1.iconBubble** (prioritizing strict lattice consistency over per-surface optimization). All 4 prose Qs resolved; structural decisions locked entirely in prose before V1 drafted.

### V1 mockup spans destination hero surface identity (Frame C picked)

V1 mockup `docs/mockups/find-destination-hero-v1.html` spans 3 frames on the one remaining structural axis (how the surface reads): **Frame A — Anchored card** (subtle refined wrap, today's structure unified, 2.5:1 map inside card) / **Frame B — Distinctive secondary hero** (paper-warm bg + soft lift + tracked small-caps eyebrow, 2:1 map bleeds edge-to-edge) / **Frame C — Map-led composition** (16:9 map fills top of card; mall + booth info as strip beneath; eyebrow floats outside above card). Each frame shows full page composition so cohesion can be evaluated end-to-end. 7-axis trade-off matrix at bottom. **David picked Frame C**.

### Pre-implementation fill-refinement prose pass (V2 skipped per `feedback_v2_options_before_drafting` ✅ Promoted-via-memory at session 135)

After Frame C pick, surfaced 4 prose Qs on fill-refinement axes (eyebrow placement / map aspect / card lift / tap surface model) instead of drafting V2 HTML mockup. All axes prose-resolvable; locked in single round. **David picked all 4 Recommended options**: eyebrow outside above card (italic Cormorant 18 + PiStorefront 18), 16:9 map aspect (~211px on iPhone SE), v2.surface.card bg + 1px border + subtle shadow (gentle lift), 3 independent tap targets (map → /map, mall subtitle → Apple Maps, vendor/booth strip → /shelf).

### 5 NEW Tech Rule candidate patterns (single firings, all promote on 2nd firing)

1. **Hybrid prose-and-exploratory ask handled via "lock prose-resolvable parts first, mockup only the exploratory axis"** — when user surfaces N concerns where some are clearly prosaically directed and some are openly exploratory, separate them: lock the prosaically-directed via prose Qs first; reserve V1 mockup for the genuinely-exploratory axes only. Sub-pattern of `feedback_pre_mockup_prose_model_first` ✅ Promoted extended from "all-prose ask" to "hybrid ask." Session 170's 4 concerns: items 1–3 prose-locked before V1; item 4 (cohesion synthesis) explored via V1 frames.
2. **Page CTA reframing dissolves a button pair into corner-bubble + tappable-card structural pair** — when "we need a primary CTA + a secondary nav" was solved as a button pair (session 169 round 2), reframe can dissolve both: primary CTA on photograph corner bubble (lattice-canonical engagement vocabulary); secondary nav as tappable component card (structural affordance). Both affordances preserved without losing discoverability; CTA-pair-class-collision dissolves. Sub-pattern of `feedback_surface_locked_design_reversals` — canonical resolution shape for "Round N button pair → Round N+1 structural dissolve."
3. **Wholesale function retirement via sed when 326-LOC block is uniquely identifiable** — when Edit's old_string match becomes impractical at multi-hundred-LOC scale, sed with line ranges is the cleaner tool. **Pair with immediate tsc check** to catch off-by-one (which DID happen this session — wasRecentPopstate's closing brace got deleted by my sed; tsc caught it in 1 round per `feedback_visibility_tools_first`). Sub-pattern of `feedback_kill_bug_class_after_3_patches` extended from bug-class to deletion-class — sed is the right tool but trust-but-verify via the boundary-gate.
4. **JSX comment at top of return body breaks the parse** — `return (\n  {/* comment */}\n  <div>...` is invalid because the first non-whitespace after `return (` must be a JSX element/expression, not a comment. Fix: move comment to JS `//` outside the return body, or place inside the JSX wrapper. Caught this session's Arc 1 padding-edit; tsc surfaced in 1 round.
5. **3-anchor page composition as the cohesion target** — when a page has compounded into N stacked sections from additive ships, the cohesion fix is to identify which sections SHOULD be one anchor + collapse them. /find/[id] went 7 sections → 3 anchors via destination hero unification. Pattern: identify "anchors" (semantic load-bearing zones) and force everything to belong to an anchor. Sub-pattern of `feedback_recurring_phrase_signals_system` ✅ Promoted, extended from "naming the system concern" to "naming the structural fix shape that collapses additive accumulation."

## ✅ Session 168 (2026-05-16) — Foundation unification (greens + inks + bg) + BottomNav pill restructure + 9 iPhone-QA-driven dial rounds — 16 runtime commits + 1 close (rotated to mini-block session 169 close)

Tagged `v0.168.0`.** NEW MEMORY PROMOTED at 4 firings: [`feedback_module_scope_cache_for_warm_nav_hydration.md`](memory/feedback_module_scope_cache_for_warm_nav_hydration.md) — when async-state hooks flash INITIAL_STATE on warm-nav mount, add module-scope cache for synchronous hydration. - **NEW (session 161): 5 Tech Rule candidate patterns observed (single firings, all promote on 2nd firing)**: (1) Web Mercator pixels-per-meter bridge for non-CSS-API consumer — Mapbox `setPaintProperty` doesn't resolve CSS vars (session 156 pattern) AND Mapbox's pixel-space concepts don't carry geographic semantics; `tenMilesInPixels(zoom, lat)` extends the "bridge at the seam" pattern from CSS var resolution to geographic radius calculation. (2) CSS variable + zoom-listener for cross-render-domain communication — TreehouseMap (React) writes `entry.el.style.setProperty('--pulse-diameter-px', ...)` on map zoom events; UserLocationPin's pulse span reads `width: var(--pulse-diameter-px)`. Avoids re-rendering UserLocationPin via createRoot on every zoom frame; CSS-var update is cheap. General pattern: when component A (React) needs to drive style on component B (rendered via createRoot/portal/marker), CSS variables on the shared parent DOM node are a cleaner bridge than imperative ref-setting or React re-render. (3) `resetKey` counter as effect re-trigger when deps don't change — when an effect's primary deps haven't changed semantically but the user wants a fresh re-run, add a `resetKey: number` prop forwarded to effect deps. Bumping the key forces re-run without faking changes to the real deps; cleaner than forwardRef + imperative handle. (4) Single coupled commit when card-geometry + shelf-math + fitBounds-padding all track the same physical dimension — extension of session 132/148 pattern. (5) Shelf-aware fitBounds padding as primitive pattern — `padding.bottom = chrome_height_in_map_coords` for any fixed-chrome-over-map scenario.

- **NEW (session 156): 12-session-deep silent Mapbox regression diagnosed + fixed at the seam** — session 144's Layer 1 token refactor moved `v1.basemap.*` tokens from literal hex strings to CSS var references (e.g., `"var(--th-v1-basemap-cream)"`). `TreehouseMap.tsx:52` calls `map.setPaintProperty(id, "background-color", v1.basemap.cream)` — Mapbox GL JS doesn't resolve CSS variables (they're a stylesheet-time concept), so the invalid value gets silently caught by the per-layer try/catch + the map keeps its default light-v11 palette. Bug masked across sessions 144-155 (no Mapbox-touching changes in the window besides session 155's value-tweak which was painting an unused token; session 145's "clean walk" Arc 5 QA covered chrome surfaces + LeafBubblePin token, not the cartographic palette). Fix in commit `f1842ab`: `resolveCssVar(value)` helper walks `var(--...)` references back to their `:root` computed value via `getComputedStyle`; pre-resolves all 6 basemap tokens at function entry. **Mapbox is the only consumer in the project that doesn't resolve CSS vars natively** — bridge lives at the seam, not at the token layer.
- **NEW (session 156): Defensive Mapbox load reliability primitive** — commit `b9576ec` ships 3 structural fixes when symptom could be any of 3 layers (container-size race during drawer animation, post-init geometry changes from iOS Safari URL bar collapse/expand, silent style.load failure from token URL restriction rejecting tile fetches on preview origins). Pattern: `map.resize()` inside `style.load` handler + `ResizeObserver` watching container + 7s watchdog `setTimeout` — if `styleLoadedRef.current` still false, surface visible "Map didn't load. Tap to retry." overlay with pill-styled Retry CTA matching MapControlPill secondary-style vocabulary. Tap fires `initKey` bump, useEffect cleanup tears down broken map + re-init creates fresh one. **Reusable for any future async-init component** — the watchdog-+-retry pattern is the canonical iOS PWA equivalent of console-error message.
- **NEW (session 156): Masthead hairline-on-scroll retire + 42-net-line dead-state cleanup** — commit `30d5296` retires the conditional `borderBottom: 1px solid v1.inkHairline | transparent` paint between masthead + content per David: *"remove the thin line under the masthead on scroll. - **NEW (session 156): Mapbox token URL allowlist operational gap** — token URL restrictions allowlist `app.kentuckytreehouse.com + localhost` only (per session 107 config). Mapbox dashboard rejects `*` wildcard patterns in the URL restriction field. Preview deployments at `*.vercel.app` fail tile fetches silently. - **NEW (session 156): 5 Tech Rule candidate patterns observed (single firings, all promote on 2nd firing)**: (1) "CSS variable string passed to non-CSS API (Mapbox setPaintProperty) — bridge at the seam, not at the token layer" — generalization of session 144's Layer 1 refactor: any consumer that doesn't use CSS-stylesheet resolution needs a `resolveCssVar` helper at the seam. (2) "Visible retry affordance as iOS PWA equivalent of console-error message" — when Inspector access is gated, shipping a visible self-diagnosing failure state in the UI is the canonical primitive. (3) "Token URL allowlist as cross-environment friction — production-only QA acceptable as fallback" — generalizes to any third-party API with URL-restricted credentials. (4) "Doc-rot comment masquerading as prop usage on broad grep" — sub-pattern of `feedback_verify_primitive_contract_via_grep` extended to dead-prop audits; refine grep (`scrollTarget=` with equals sign) before declaring a prop in use. (5) "12-session-deep silent regression diagnosed in 2 round-trips via screenshot + code read" — silent regressions in design-system-token consumers can persist across many sessions until visual QA + a comparison against another rendering surfaces the divergence.

- **RESOLVED (session 110→134): Home masonry right-column slide-down on entrance** ✅ closed via session-134 commit `5d70c75`. Bug class was a two-paint sequence: column-2 marginTop initialized at SKELETON_OFFSET (70, useState init guess correct for skeleton's 4:5 photo-only tile) → useEffect runs AFTER browser paints → measure() updates state to actual ~100–120px (real tile = 4:5 photo + relative-timestamp "below" row + polaroid mat padding) → second paint snaps to new offset. Browser's snap between two paints reads as a slide-down animation even though no CSS transition is set. Single useEffect → useLayoutEffect swap lands the measurement in the first paint; ResizeObserver registration unchanged (first tile's height can still shift post-mount). 24-session-deep carry retires.

- **NEW PRIMARY (session 93): iPhone QA of Wave 1 follow-up commits still owed.** David QA'd /login triage flow this session but session-92 follow-up surfaces (contact mailto, mall hero composition, EditBoothSheet hero section, /shelves admin EditBoothSheet hero controls) remain un-walked. Watch-items per session 92 close still apply.
- **NEW (session 93): R1 (shopper accounts) routing slot pre-baked.** Login routing model anticipates the R1 shape: `/login` triage page has 2 cards today; R1 adds a 3rd "I'm shopping" card. `/login/email` Screen 2 title "Vendor Sign in" generalizes to "Sign in" when R1 ships. The "Just shopping?" guest disambiguation line on /login retires (replaced by 3rd card). Subtitle generalizes. All 4 changes contained to `app/login/page.tsx` + `app/login/email/page.tsx`.
- **NEW (session 93): /admin/login + /setup `handleGoToLogin` callsites left routing through triage.** Bare `/login` calls — go through triage cards. If user testing reveals friction (extra tap to reach the form for what feels like a known returning user), single-line update each to point at `/login/email` directly.
- **NEW (session 93): Triage-first routing for ambiguous-state pages.** First firing — `/login` had to handle 4 user states (returning vendor / new vendor / authed / magic-link callback) which a single form could not disambiguate. Pattern: when a page must serve genuinely-different user states, surface the disambiguation in routing rather than letting one component conditionally render. Tech Rule on second firing.
- **NEW (session 93): Inbound deep-link audit when splitting a route.** First firing — when changing route topology (one route → two routes), grep all inbound references and decide per-callsite whether to update or rely on forwarding. /vendor-request "Sign in instead" + /my-shelf re-auth bounce got per-callsite upgrades. Tech Rule on second firing.
- **NEW (session 93): Forward-known-states + render-fresh-states routing primitive.** First firing — `/login` triage state machine: if `?confirmed=1` → render polling, if explicit redirect → forward, if authed → forward, else → render triage cards. Pattern: render only states that need fresh interaction; forward known states to their canonical destination. Tech Rule on second firing.
